 tamilnadu kii raajnneeti ke pitamah em karunanidhi kaa mangalvaar ko chennai main nidhan ho gaya

 karunanidhi kareeb 19 saal tak tamilnadu ke siem rahe or unki raajnneeti main jati, afrmative ection, panth nirpekshata, kshetreey pahchaan jaise vichaaron kaa gaharaa asar tha
 Karunanidhi was born into a backward caste family
 apni kishoravastha main hi vah periyar i
 V
 ramasami ke saamaajik nyaay andolan main shaamil ho gaye the
 In the first fifty years of the twentieth century, Periyar's anti-caste extremist views created a political boil in the Tamil-speaking areas of the then Madras Presidency
 indian express ke mutabik unhonejatigat vibhedaur oonch-neech ko maanane se inkaar karte hue dravin pahchaan ko aage badhaate hue tamil bhashaa, samskruti ke gaurav par jor diya

 ve to yahaan tak maanate the ki aazaadee mil bhi gai to dakshin bharat par brahmanon ke prabhutv vaale congress kaa hi shashan hoga
 These revolutionary ideas of Periyar created a stir in the social relations of the entire Tamil region
 periyar karunanidhi ke guru the
 Karunanidhi's political understanding and stature grew as a young follower of Periyar and the founder of DMK and an associate of Tamil Nadu's first CM CN Annadurai
 periyar bharat kii aazaadee se sahamat nahin the or iskaa virodh kar rahe the
 But Annadurai joined the politics of the country after independence keeping a different opinion from them
 karunanidhi bhi annadurai ke saath diemke ke sansthaapakon main se the
 The entire Dravidian movement was anti-caste
 annadurai kaa naaraa tha 'ondre kulam, oruvane devan' (ek maanavtaa, ek ishwar)
 During his tenure as the Chief Minister, Karunanidhi began to implement the idea of the Dravin movement that he had met with his guru
 desh main sabase pehle jatigat aarakshan lagu karne vaale rajyon main madras presidency tha
 The DMK was originally founded on the legacy of the Justice Party and Periyar's self-respect movement
 isliye diemke ne sadiyon tak vanchit rahe samudaay ko aarakshan ke dwaara shashakt banane kaa prayaas kiya
 Karunanidhi tried to represent every section of society at every level in administration
 haalanki unke aalochak yah aarope lagaate rahe hai ki unhone jati ko vot bank kii raajnneeti main badal diya
